## Domain Knowledge
**Domain**: nonlinear oscillator dynamics
**Analysis**: This task involves finding the acceleration (dv/dt) of a nonlinear harmonic oscillator as a function of position x, velocity v, and time t. The acceleration in such systems typically arises from restoring forces (functions of x) and damping forces (functions of v), possibly with nonlinear terms like cubic restoring forces (Duffing oscillator) or nonlinear damping (van der Pol oscillator).

**Common formula structures** (built-in generic + LLM domain-specific):
- Arrhenius equation: k = c0 * exp(c1 / T) (chemical reaction rate dependence on temperature)
- Coulomb's / Newton's inverse-square law: F = c0 / r**2 (gravitational or electrostatic force)
- Stefan-Boltzmann law: P = c0 * T**4 (blackbody radiation power vs temperature)
- Beer-Lambert law: I = c0 * exp(c1 * x) (light intensity attenuation through a medium)
- Michaelis-Menten kinetics: v = c0 * S / (S + c1) (enzyme-catalyzed reaction saturation)
- Hill equation: y = c0 * x**c1 / (x**c1 + c2) (cooperative binding, sigmoidal dose-response)
- Kepler's third law: T**2 = c0 * a**3 (orbital period vs semi-major axis)
- Newton's law of cooling: T = c0 + c1 * exp(c2 * t) (exponential thermal relaxation)
- Clausius-Clapeyron relation: log(P) = c0 + c1 / T (vapor pressure vs temperature)
- Langmuir adsorption isotherm: theta = c0 * P / (1 + c1 * P) (surface adsorption equilibrium)
- Freundlich isotherm: q = c0 * C**c1 (empirical adsorption on heterogeneous surface)
- Stokes' drag: F = c0 * r * v (viscous drag force on a sphere in fluid)
- Logistic growth: N = c0 / (1 + c1 * exp(c2 * t)) (population dynamics with carrying capacity)
- Planck-Wien approximation: I = c0 * f**3 * exp(c1 * f / T) (thermal radiation spectrum)
- Simple harmonic oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x (linear restoring force)
- Damped harmonic oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * v (linear restoring + linear damping)
- Duffing oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**3 (cubic nonlinear restoring force)
- Damped Duffing oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**3 + c2 * v (cubic restoring + linear damping)
- Van der Pol oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * (1 - c2 * x**2) * v (nonlinear damping dependent on position)
- Quintic nonlinear oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**3 + c2 * x**5 (higher-order restoring force)
- Nonlinear damping: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * v * abs(v) (quadratic velocity-dependent damping)
- Cubic damping oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * v**3 (cubic velocity damping)
- Driven nonlinear oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**3 + c2 * sin(c3 * t) (periodic external forcing)
- Softening/hardening spring: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**2 (quadratic nonlinearity, asymmetric potential)
- Full Duffing with damping and drive: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**3 + c2 * v + c3 * cos(c4 * t) (complete Duffing equation)
- Position-velocity coupling: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x * v (mixed nonlinear coupling term)
- Parametric oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * (1 + c1 * cos(c2 * t)) * x (time-modulated stiffness)
- Rayleigh oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * v + c2 * v**3 (Rayleigh-type nonlinear damping)

**Formula structure heuristic features**:
- Oscillation damping envelope â†’ Exponential decay envelope f(x)*exp(-c*Abs(x)) for symmetric damped oscillation, Gaussian envelope f(x)*exp(-c*x**2) for localized wave packets
- Saturation/clipping effects â†’ Rational fraction x/(1+x), tanh; for variables with alternating positive/negative in oscillatory systems, selectively apply Abs
- Growth/decay â†’ Exponential growth exp(c*t), Logistic 1/(1+exp(-c*x)), power law x**c
- Threshold/activation behavior â†’ Max(x-c, 0), piecewise functions
- Coupling/cross effects â†’ Product terms between variables x*y, power-law coupling x**c1 * y**c2
- Odd-power restoring forces (x, x**3, x**5) â†’ symmetric potential wells preserving oscillation symmetry
- Velocity-dependent terms proportional to v â†’ linear energy dissipation or injection (damping/anti-damping)
- Terms like x**2 * v or (1 - x**2) * v â†’ amplitude-dependent damping characteristic of self-sustained oscillators (van der Pol type)
- Cubic position term x**3 with opposite sign to linear term â†’ Duffing-type hardening or softening spring behavior
- Sinusoidal functions of time sin(c*t) or cos(c*t) â†’ external periodic driving forces
- Even-power position terms (x**2) â†’ asymmetric restoring force breaking reflection symmetry
- Products x*v â†’ nonlinear coupling between position and velocity indicating non-conservative or gyroscopic effects
- Absence of explicit time dependence â†’ autonomous system with conserved or dissipated energy

sin and exp can't replicate log(|v|+1).

**Candidate 39:** `c0*x + c1*x^3 + c2 + c3*sin(t) + c4*v + c5*log(c6*exp(c7*v)+1)`
Set c0=0, c2=0. Then: `c1*x^3 + c3*sin(t) + c4*v + c5*log(c6*exp(c7*v)+1)`.
`log(c6*exp(c7*v)+1)` is a softplus-like function. For this to equal `log(|v|+1)`, we'd need `c5*log(c6*exp(c7*v)+1) + c4*v = -0.826v - 0.413*log(|v|+1)`.
The softplus `log(A*exp(Bv)+1)` is smooth and monotonic, while `log(|v|+1)` has a kink at v=0. These can't be equal.
Candidate 39 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 40:** `c0*v*x + c2*Abs(v)^(1/3) + v/(c1+v) + c3*x^3 + c4*sin(t)`
Has cross term v*x and `Abs(v)^(1/3)`.
Candidate 40 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 41:** `c0*x + c1*x^3 + c2*sin(t) + c3*v + c4*log(c5*exp(c6*v)+1)`
Same as 39 analysis. Softplus can't match log(|v|+1).
Candidate 41 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 42:** `(c0*v*sin(c1*v+c2) + c3 + v - (c4+v)*(c5*x^3+c6*sin(t)))/(c4+v)`

Has complicated v-dependent terms.

= `c0*v + c2*sin(c3*v+c4) + (c5+v)/(c1+v) - c6*sin(t) - c7*x^3`
Has sin(c3*v+c4) and rational v terms.
Candidate 43 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 44:** `c0*x^3 + c1*sin(t) + c2*v^4 + c3*exp(c4*v) + c5*log(v+1) + c6*v`
Has `log(v+1)` not `log(|v|+1)`. Since v takes both positive and negative values, `log(v+1)` is undefined for v < -1, while `log(|v|+1)` is always defined. These are different functions even where both are defined (for v<0: log(v+1) â‰  log(-v+1)).
Candidate 44 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 45:** `c0*(c1*(c2*log(c3*exp(c4*v)+1) + c5*x^3 + c6*sin(t)) + c7 + v)`
= `c0*c1*c2*log(c3*exp(c4*v)+1) + c0*c1*c5*x^3 + c0*c1*c6*sin(t) + c0*c7 + c0*v`
= `A*log(B*exp(C*v)+1) + D*x^3 + E*sin(t) + F + G*v`
Softplus can't match log(|v|+1).
Candidate 45 verdict: [NO MATCH]
